rel="nofollow">10.1098/rstb.2007.0030</a>. <a href="/wiki/PubMed_Central" title="PubMed Central">PMC</a> <span class="cs1-lock-free" title="Freely accessible"><a class="external text" <li id="cite_note-Fargione08-46"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-Fargione08_46-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Fargione08_46-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation journal">Fargione; Hill, J; Tilman, D; Polasky, S; Hawthorne, P;  et al. (2008-02-29). <a class="external text" href="http://www.sciencemag.org/cgi/content/abstract/1152747" rel="nofollow">"Land Clearing and the Biofuel Carbon Debt"</a>. <i><a href="/wiki/Science_(journal)" title="Science (journal)">Science</a></i>. <b>319</b> (5867): 1235–1238. <a href="/wiki/Bibcode" title="Bibcode">Bibcode</a>:<a class="external text" href="http://adsabs.harvard.edu/abs/2008Sci...319.1235F" rel="nofollow">2008Sci...319.1235F</a>. <a href="/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" title="Digital object identifier">doi</a>:<a class="external text" href="//doi.org/10.1126%2Fscience.1152747" rel="nofollow">10.1126/science.1152747</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/PubMed_Identifier" title="PubMed Identifier">PMID</a> <a class="external text" href="//www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/18258862" rel="nofollow">18258862</a><span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">2009-06-09</span></span>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Science&amp;rft.atitle=Land+Clearing+and+the+Biofuel+Carbon+Debt&amp;rft.volume=319&amp;rft.issue=5867&amp;rft.pages=1235-1238&amp;rft.date=2008-02-29&amp;rft_id=info%3Apmid%2F18258862&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.1126%2Fscience.1152747&amp;rft_id=info%3Abibcode%2F2008Sci...319.1235F&amp;rft.au=Fargione&amp;rft.au=Hill%2C+J&amp;rft.au=Tilman%2C+D&amp;rft.au=Polasky%2C+S&amp;rft.au=Hawthorne%2C+P&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.sciencemag.org%2Fcgi%2Fcontent%2Fabstract%2F1152747&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AIndirect+land+use+change+impacts+of+biofuels"></span><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/> <i>Originally published online in Science Express on 7 February 2008, available <a class="external text" href="http://www.nature.org/initiatives/climatechange/files/land_clearing_and_the_biofuel_carbon_debt.pdf" rel="nofollow">here</a></i>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-47"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-47">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><i>"For example, using Searchinger’s “indirect analysis” approach you can “prove” that increasing the mileage standards for vehicles contributes to global warming. Consider: Every gallon of gasoline not used by a motorist saves him $3.50 at today’s prices. He can use that money to buy other things. For example, at current prices (about $80 per ton), $3.50 could buy him about 90 pounds of coal. Burning that coal would obviously produce far more carbon dioxide emissions than burning the 6 pounds of carbon in one gallon of gas. So higher mileage standards for cars cause global warming. Q.E.D."</i>, in: <cite class="citation book">Zubrin, Robert (2012). <i>Merchants of Despair: Radical Environmentalists, Criminal Pseudo-Scientists, and the Fatal Cult of Antihumanism</i>. New Atlantis Books. <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1594034763" title="Special:BookSources/978-1594034763">978-1594034763</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Merchants+of+Despair%3A+Radical+Environmentalists%2C+Criminal+Pseudo-Scientists%2C+and+the+Fatal+Cult+of+Antihumanism&amp;rft.pub=New+Atlantis+Books&amp;rft.date=2012&amp;rft.isbn=978-1594034763&amp;rft.au=Zubrin%2C+Robert&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AIndirect+land+use+change+impacts+of+biofuels"></span><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/></span>
